115018637823093019663</userid>
<user_name>Kute KittyKat Productions< /user_name><Time>1600835548259</Time>< rating>
5</rating>
<text>Finally, Oakley has a kebab restaurant!

We decided to try a selection of dishes.

The pizza crust is deliciously chewy and smoky. It‚Äôs the best crust I‚Äôve had at any local pizza place. The sauce and toppings are presented nicely but are about average in taste and selection.

The chicken wings were juicy but otherwise also average. It‚Äôs nice to get carrots as well as celery with wings, but I wish they were hand cut spears, rather than those kiddie-style baby carrots.

Where Oakley Tavern shines is their kebabs.

We had each kind: Chicken, Beef, and Chapli. These are truly excellent dishes. The meat is well-seasoned and grilled perfectly, with a lovely char. The standout is the Chapli. I don‚Äôt ordinarily enjoy grilled mince because it can tend towards dryness. These were astoundingly good - the best I‚Äôve ever had, anywhere. They were flavorful and very, very tender. This is a dish you could make your name with. Well done!

The rice is a fancy basmati. I believe it might be called the ‚Äòsella‚Äô type. The grains are long, plump, have a nice bite, and a naturally buttery flavor. Eating the rice with the meat juices soaking in was pure pleasure.

The Potato-Pea Curry, Green Chutney, and Salata accompaniments were bright and fresh. The Yogurt Sauce was also very good. Whatever yogurt is being used to make this, please don‚Äôt change it.

The bread that came with was advertised as naan but it more resembles a thin focaccia. A traditional, chewy, fire-roasted naan would go better. But otherwise, these kebab dishes were flawless.

They‚Äôre a new restaurant and are experiencing some operational teething pains. It was chaotic, and we only visited on a Tuesday. I can‚Äôt imagine weekend dinner rushes there. One of my items was not packed in my to-go order and so I had to go back for it. There was a lot of hectic running back and forth in the restaurant. They have plenty of staff - who are lovely, friendly, and helpful - but there is a lack of organization. An experienced Expediter is needed to orchestrate things to run smoothly and ensure accuracy. And they need to clarify their menu offerings and make it easy for customers to access. A link to their website and a current menu are essential.

Their kebab meals are outstanding. I sincerely hope that they work out these operational kinks because I want very much for them to succeed. (And I hope they add lamb kebabs to their menu soon! Without lamb, it kind of feels like something is missing. Lamb kebabs, please!!)

<Rating>4< /Rating>< Text>
Good place for a quick bite. Only had their tacos here and once had their caldo de res. Meat is always good - carnitas, asada, lengua. I mostly come for their lengua tacos which are tender and moist. Today four lengua tacos and a Mexican coca cola cost me a little more than $11.

The interior is not much to speak of and it's not the type of place where you would lounge. Thus, I always order take out. That said the staff is polite, talkative at times and quick.

I think there is only street parking and that is normally filled up in front of the shop. Note that if you do park on the street, South Street is pretty busy so be careful as you exit your car.<//Text>

I looked at several "custom build" companies online, and decided on Cyberpower.  It appeared that they were building quality "custom" computers at a more reasonable price then several other sites.  Plus, they had a number of free upgrades available that would give my PC more power for the price.  I was amazed at just how much control I had over just about every component, including the case.  I finally decided on the Black Pearl, and began customizing.  I had to compromise a few times to stay within my budget, but in the end I was more than satisfied with the result.  Being able to save and print out my specs was great.  Ordering was easy, and they kept me updated by emails through each step, all the way to my doorstep.  I had no problems setting it up.  Everything works great and it is amazingly quiet.  I took 1/2 star off because one of the fans has started to make a slight clicking noise, and 1/2 star off because the "gaming" keyboard that came with it was flimsy and nowhere near the quality of the computer.  I've bought a better keyboard.  So, would I recommend Cyberpower to others?  Absolutely!  In fact, I already have!</review>

Spencer Huff<//Name>
<Review>I first heard of CyberpowerPC from a website that gave ratings of the best computers for video games for 2012. Their site is easy to use, their customer service is always available and ready to help, and they even have a rather active user-forum that you can use if you have trouble with your computer.

There's a wide-range of parts and components available when constructing your computer, but it varies as to how wide that supply pool goes for each option. On the short end of the spectrum, I found it frustrating that Cyberpower doesn't offer all of their available components - such as CPUs and power supplies - for every different "build" that Cyberpower offers. On the other hand, the range of options available for motherboards was absolutely staggering. This leads me to my next point.

Although the site is user-friendly, it's not very friendly for those who are not in-the-know regarding PC components. I found choosing a motherboard for my PC to be extremely difficult for this reason - I had to independently research every single option that Cyberpower offered before I picked one.

Ultimately, however, I'm extremely satisfied with my new machine. It's able to run any game I throw at it with absolute ease and at the highest of graphical settings.

Although it's somewhat pricier to order a computer from Cyberpower than if you were to build it yourself (and that's true no matter who you order a custom-built PC from), Cyberpower has the lowest of prices out of all the vendors that I've seen.

They also have usually have lots of deals available too - things like free video card upgrades, special video game offers, free high-end gaming mice and keyboards, etc.

So if you're going to order a custom-built PC, you should look no further than Cyberpower."<//Review><resp>None< /resp>< Pictures>

< Text>
I was in the market for a new computer and decided to get a custom build to fit all my needs. I shopped around online for a while, reading reviews and comparing prices. I decided on going with Cyberpower because the reviews on the work were highly rated, and the only negatives I really found was the lack of communication when a part is back ordered. I know that no business is perfect so if that's the worst case scenario at least I knew what to expect.

I ordered my dream build and expected to have my new computer shipped in two weeks. Instead, no progress was shown for three weeks. I contacted customer service, inquiring about the progress on my build. They informed me that they were waiting on my optical drive to come in. And my computer would be sent out at the end of the week.
Cons: (I have to agree with another review I saw about the lack of customer service.) Although they did respond to my inquiry in a timely manner, I personally would have appreciated the courtesy of being contacted if there was a problem. Paying over a thousand dollars for a product or service should automatically entitle me to be the first to be informed if there is a hold up or problem with my order. If they address this issue they will be even more successful.
Pros:
After the optical drive came in, the process seemed to progress quickly. Almost a month after ordering, I received my highly anticipated custom built computer. It was beautiful. They did everything I requested and added all the parts I ordered. They packaged it with care and it arrived when expected. I would definitely recommend CyberpowerPC for your next build. I am ecstatic about my super computer. There work is top notch.<//Text>

< review>
I just recently purchased a Cyberpower Black Pearl gaming desktop. Prior to my purchase, I was having heat and power issues with my ASUS G73J gaming notebook, and I needed a more reliable computer. I had read a number of reviews and recommendations of gaming desktops, and the Cyberpower Black Pearl appeared to be the best combination of cost vs. performance.

Ordering from Cyberpower online initially seemed daunting when first examining all the options and upgrades available, but I phoned their sales support department and they were very helpful in clarifying my choices and requirements.

I chose a system that met my needs, selected a number of cooling and drive upgrades, made my purchase, and received the computer faster than Cyperpower promised.

So far the PC is performing admirably, the only complaint or issue I have is that there is very little support or installation documentation - none for the overall system and mostly just the vendor component supplied literature.</review>

I received emails every single step of the way, from confirmation of order, to the build in progress, to quality control, and finally to your order has shipped. Based on my experiences from beginning to end, I will definitely be going back to CyberPower for my computing needs.< /text>

<user_name>Joseph Scudellari< /user_name><Text>It's been around 10 months since I bought my Cyberpower PC Fangbook X7-100, and everything's going well. So far, there have been no problems to report. During the buying process, Cyberpower's customer service helped keep me in touch with my order's status and answered my questions. The assembly to delivery period was a bit extensive -- about 2 weeks longer than their estimate -- but very much worth the wait. I've loved every minute of using this beast, and I have divided my review into categories below.

‚Ä¢ Performance: 5/5

Wonderfully fast with its i7 3630qm quad core processor, as long as you don't clog your hard drive full with data or multitask with too many intensive programs open at once. No complaints speed wise; it rivals my desktop in speed.

‚Ä¢ Gaming: 4.5/5

Rocking the Nvidia GTX 675MX, although no longer top by today's standards, I can play even the latest games on high to ultra settings while keeping a smooth framerate -- somewhere around 50-60 fps.The chassis and internal parts keep cool under stress from hard gaming sessions. Combining the built-in heatsinks and gpu fan with an external laptop cooler keeps temps below 65 degrees Celsius while running games such as Skyrim and Battlefield 3 on ultra.

‚Ä¢ Ergonomics: 4.5/5

The dashboard's sleek aluminum finish is very comfortable, although the touchpad is a little bit flimsy-feeling. I've got a gaming mouse hooked up, though, so normally, the touchpad isn't any issue at all. Fangbook's keyboard feels smooth and typing is easy with the chiclet key design. I've compared typing on my Fang to typing on a Mac and they feel quite similar, which is a great bonus.

‚Ä¢ Sound and Screen: 4/5

One of the few things not up to par with the rest of the machine. The speakers' sound output sounds a little -- how should I describe it -- harsh... It doesn't sound quite clear cut. Detail is there, but just not presented with enough gusto and clarity.
The Fang's screen is above average. It's got a good viewing angle, so you can still see objects onscreen in detail even when viewing the screen from an obtuse angle. Colors represent themselves well enough, maybe a bit muted in some cases. All in all, respectable and definitely fine for watching movies and other forms of media. You can also adjust brightness, contrast, and vibrancy in your Intel HD graphics control panel.

‚Ä¢ Extras: 5/5

The programmable and function buttons above the keyboard allow for quick activation or deactivation of certain settings and actions, such as toggling my GPU fan, opening up my disk drive, or turning on the Fangbook's backlit keyboard. Seeing the keys accented by a menacing red light while sitting in a dark room not only looks great, but aids typing.

To sum it all up, its been almost ten months and there have been no problems at all. I'm extremely happy with my purchase thus far and hope the smooth sailing continues.< /Text>< Pictures>

I used to shop at BestBuy for all my computer needs, and recently purchased a Surface Pro and low-end laptop before that. I spend enough there that I'm an elite member. While I will continue to shop there, I think I will be getting all of my computer-related things from Cyber-Power PC from now on.

I don't base my customer loyalty on a single purchase, so I expect to be impressed in the future as well, but first impressions are everything and this one swept me off my feet.

Here is my basic rating for everything, with specific comments:
(1-10: ten is best)

Pricing 10/10:
Best price I could find by several hundred dollars. While I mentioned several other large purchases around the same time, I want to mention that I do NOT like to spend beyond my means. The price I got put me under my target without sacrificing the hardware, and I cannot tell you how exciting that felt.

Shipping 10/10:
They note that it can take up to two weeks for the item to make it out to you. It took one week. The pc was packed with just the level of care I expected. There is nothing that blew me away here, but it was still as good as I could imagine given what I ordered.

Ease of Use 8/10:
I found it a little frustrating, when setting up my PC, that I couldn't make my choices and then save the choices I had already made to come back to; sort of as a "Draft" of my new PC. I had to re-make my PC 3 times due to this data not being saved. Although the functionality may be there, but I just didn't see it.

Also, the layout is very user-friendly, but there really should have been some more detailed information for each of the options I was choosing for my PC. The information there was sub-par, and I needed to google for more details to make an informed choice.

Overall Experience 10/10:
The amount of good will earned by the quality of the product and the price along with great service (shipping) has made this the best large purchase I've made in a long time. It eclipses the minor frustrations in the setting up of my PC for purchase.

I recommend you at least build your PC, and compare it to your other options. I think you will find a gem in there.<//Review>

This was my first purchase at CyberpowerPC and I am truly amazed by the quality of the system I received.

I used to work parttime as a system administrator for our university, where we always ordered our PCs from DELL. During this time I had issues with those PCs ranging from loose USB sockets on the mainboard to buggy power saving modes. This issues were not very frequent, but nevertheless they were present. We continued to order from DELL, since we did not know a better reseller for business computers that would meet our budget.

The quality of my recent purchase from cyberpowerpc lets me think we should have bought our PCs from cyberpowerpc. The quality of assembly was what surprised me most. Since the price  was so incredibly cheap with respect to the quality of components ordered, I expected a hastily assembled system. However what I received outshined everything I have ever seen. You think DELL does a good job with cable management and assembly? No they don't, cyberpowerpc does! This was the most carefully assembled system I have ever seen. Truly awesome! I bet this PC will run for years without the slightest issue. This PC surpassed all my expectations!

Also you know those rebate programs? Were you send in the original barcode label from the packaging? Cyberpowerpc cut out every single barcode label for which a rebate was available and attached it to the shipment. This way I was able to save an additional 90 Dollars.

I also want to comment on some of the problems, I had read about before ordering. There were reviewers writing of defect or loose hardware when they got their system. I went with the special care shipping, where they insert an additional foam to protect the components from coming loose. It worked perfectly. We all know how shipment companies handle packages. If something is loose when arriving, it is most likely not the fault of cyberpowerpc. I would definitely recommend to choose this slightly more expensive shipment option.

Also some people complained about bad customer service. I can't agree with that. I had to change my order a few days after submitting it, which was no problem at all. The customer service was very friendly and applied the changes immediately.

To sum up, I would like to say that up until know, I had two companies I would always buy from. These are Kingston for memory modules and Nvidia for graphics cards. Although sometimes expensive, they proved to be exceptionally reliable and durable, which are the most important properties of computer hardware. I always buy from them, if I need one of those components. Now I have a third company. Its cyberpowerpc! Whenever I will need a complete system, I will buy from them. They are definitely worth every single dollar.</review>

< Review>
This is my first time to purchase a desktop and my colleague recommended CyberpowerPC. They offer a spectrum of fully customizable hardwares at 50% cheaper than those brand name PC manufacturers, although sometimes it becomes hard to tell which case/fans/motherboard (insert those parts that are not easily quantifiable) is better.

I ended up getting a fairly priced powerful desktop and it arrived roughly on time. The keyboard and mouse was different from what I ordered because those models were on back order and they shipped some generic ones for temporary use (the backordered ones did arrive later).

At the beginning I had some problem with the new Windows 8 as I didn't have administrator access. I reconfigured the RAID format of my hard drive and reinstalled Windows 8 with a very knowledgeable techinician on the phone. He knows everything about the system and was able to point to me exactly which button to click at every step. Now the machine is running at its full power and I'm very satisfied with it. I will definitely go to CyberpowerPC again next time when I need to upgrade.</Review>

< Text>
"Over the years I've bought pre-built systems, and built quite a few of my own. I was looking over what is available from different companies and nothing came close to what I wanted. I found CyberpowerPC by accident and their web site amazed me. The bottom line is that in a world where some companies "overcook" their motherboards for performance and "customer value" that overheat or burn up after a few years (without overclocking), finding a good system for a reasonable price that can handle high performance long term isn't easy.
The cyberpowerPC website allows a person to start with a base system with specifications they choose, and choose each and every component or option for the computer with lists and a simple selection tool that covers every last option for the system including some I had not thought of I decided I wanted.

Original documents for parts were included when appropriate (such as the motherboard). Even though as a multi-tasker I was not pleased with Windows 8 I had to admit as a person who is a "hard sell" that the system met my expectations completely which were very high based on the order and the attention to detail of the ordering system.

When I ordered my system and chose to pay extra for a rush order, sales noticed that the system couldn't be rushed any more than the usual and put a hold on my order until I could contact them and give them permission to remove the extra charge.

Due to the professionalism, the ordering system, the attention to detail on the system, and easy help from technical support resolving one simple misunderstanding about wiring I gave the company a completely excellent rating. After seeing my rating and review of their product I was asked to publish a review.

In short cyberpowerPC combines the professional assembly and attention to detail with a total choice on all parts and options for the PC. Unlike other bulk computer manufacturers they also sent me an operating system installation disk rather than ask me to create one."<//Text>

"This is my 2nd CyberpowerPC unit.
Very nicely assembled and impressive shipping protection (worth the small fee!).
This unit has the triple fan liquid cooling, which keeps the CPU at about 100 degrees F, and is nearly silent. I paid a little extra for all the "silencing" modifications, and you can barely hear this computer running!
I have the eight core AMD CPU and dual Crossfire ATI video cards, lots of memory and the 10,000 RPM hard drive, so this machine really screams playing games.
The only glitch was that the case has front accessable "hot swappable" slots for 4 hard drives. Only the one with the included hard drive was wired with an SATA cable. The other three drives were powered, but no SATA cables attached. It took longer to diagnose the issue than fix it, as I already had extra SATA cables.
That was the only issue, and I have been very happy with this order."<//Text>
